(03:22:57 PM) qwer: 兄弟们，怎么知道Nginx + uwsgi_php在运行啊
(03:23:39 PM) qwer: server {
(03:23:40 PM) qwer: #this is to avoid Request Entity Too Large error
(03:23:40 PM) qwer: client_max_body_size 1000M;
(03:23:40 PM) qwer: # deny access to some special files
(03:23:40 PM) qwer: location ~ ^/(data|config|\.ht|db_structure\.xml|README) {
(03:23:40 PM) qwer: deny all;
(03:23:42 PM) qwer: }
(03:23:44 PM) qwer: # pass all .php or .php/path urls to uWSGI
(03:23:46 PM) qwer: location ~ ^(.+\.php)(.*)$ {
(03:23:48 PM) qwer: include uwsgi_params;
(03:23:50 PM) qwer: uwsgi_modifier1 14;
(03:23:52 PM) qwer: #Uncomment line below if you get connection refused error. Remember to commet out line with "uwsgi_pass 127.0.0.1:3001;" below
(03:23:55 PM) qwer: #uwsgi_pass unix:/run/uwsgi/owncloud.sock;
(03:23:59 PM) qwer: uwsgi_pass 127.0.0.1:3001;
(03:24:01 PM) qwer: }
(03:24:03 PM) qwer: # everything else goes to the filesystem,
(03:24:05 PM) qwer: # but / will be mapped to index.php and run through uwsgi
(03:24:07 PM) qwer: location / {
(03:24:09 PM) qwer: root /home/qwer/www/owncloud;
(03:24:11 PM) qwer: index index.php;
(03:24:13 PM) qwer: rewrite ^/.well-known/carddav /remote.php/carddav/ redirect;
(03:24:15 PM) qwer: rewrite ^/.well-known/caldav /remote.php/caldav/ redirect;
(03:24:17 PM) qwer: }
(03:24:19 PM) qwer: }
(03:24:22 PM) Lisongmin: 侬刷屏了～～
